‚óŹ All tests pass. Here's what was added:

  pkg/ctxcomp/compressor.go:
  - maxDepth field on Compressor (default 1, max 3)
  - WithDepth(n) fluent setter
  - Compress now iterates level-by-level: extracts deps from fetched full
  sources at each level, tracking seen to avoid cycles
  - fetchContractsWithSources returns both contracts and full sources for deeper
   expansion

  internal/mcp/handlers_context.go:
  - depth parameter on the context analyze type (default 1)

  Usage:
  SAP(action="analyze", params={"type": "context", "object_type": "CLAS",
  "name": "ZCL_TEST", "depth": 2})

  - depth: 1 ‚ÄĒ direct deps only (current behavior)
  - depth: 2 ‚ÄĒ deps of deps
  - depth: 3 ‚ÄĒ max, three levels deep

  The maxDeps budget is shared across all levels, so it won't explode ‚ÄĒ if you
  have 20 max deps and level 1 uses 15, level 2 only gets 5 more slots. Cycles
  are prevented via the seen set.

‚óŹ OK, here's the full picture:

  What's wired into vsp MCP today:

  1. parse_abap ‚ÄĒ Go-side tokenizer + statement classifier. Basic: splits into
  tokens, classifies ~40 statement types (DATA, IF, LOOP, SELECT, METHOD, CLASS,
   etc.)
  2. analyze_deps ‚ÄĒ regex + parser-based dependency extraction with confidence
  scoring
  3. context ‚ÄĒ full dependency expansion with contract compression (now with
  depth 1-3)

  What exists on SAP ($ZOZIK):
  - zcl_lexer ‚ÄĒ full abaplint lexer (transpiled from TS), 46 token subclasses
  - zcl_statement_parser ‚ÄĒ proper statement splitting with colon chaining
  - Statement matcher (392 types) ‚ÄĒ not yet ported
  - Structure parser ‚ÄĒ not yet ported

  Re: using it as a real linter ‚ÄĒ –ī–į, –į–Ī—Ā–ĺ–Ľ—é—ā–Ĺ–ĺ –ľ–ĺ–∂–Ķ–ľ. –£ –Ĺ–į—Ā –Ķ—Ā—ā—Ć –ī–≤–į –Ņ—É—ā–ł:

  Path A: Go-side lint rules (fast, offline)

  Build lint rules on top of the existing Go tokenizer/parser. We already
  classify statements ‚ÄĒ add rules like:
  - Naming conventions: lv_ for locals, gv_ for globals, iv_/ev_/rv_ for method
  params
  - Line length: max 120 chars
  - Empty blocks: IF/ENDIF with no content
  - Obsolete statements: MOVE, COMPUTE, ADD/SUBTRACT, CALL METHOD
  - Missing TYPE: untyped DATA declarations
  - Hardcoded literals: magic numbers in logic

  Path B: SAP-side via ExecuteABAP (deep, semantic)

  Call zcl_lexer on SAP for proper tokenization + use SAP's own SCAN ABAP-SOURCE
   for semantic checks:
  - Cross-references validation
  - Actual type checking
  - Unused variables (via SCAN + symbol table)

  Recommendation

  Start with Path A ‚ÄĒ add a lint_abap analyze type that runs Go-side rules on
  the parsed AST. It's instant, works offline, and covers the most common
  convention checks. We can wire it as:

  SAP(action="analyze", params={"type": "lint_abap", "source": "...", "rules":
  ["naming", "obsolete", "line_length"]})
  SAP(action="analyze", params={"type": "lint_abap", "object_type": "CLAS",
  "name": "ZCL_TEST"})

  Want me to implement lint_abap with a starter set of rules?

‚óŹ Bash(# Check if the lexer produces Colon or if it's a later step

  ‚éŅ ¬†/tmp/abaplint/packages/core/src/abap/1_lexer/tokens/colon.ts:export cl
     ass Colon extends AbstractToken {

  Searched for 1 pattern (ctrl+o to expand)

‚óŹ Interesting ‚ÄĒ the lexer itself never emits Colon! It treats : as a split
  character but the token that gets the colon string is just Identifier. The
  Colon token type exists but is probably used in a later stage. Let me verify:

  Searched for 2 patterns (ctrl+o to expand)

‚óŹ So the lexer never creates Colon ‚ÄĒ colons become Identifier tokens. This is
  because : is in the splits map and also in bufs, so the colon itself becomes a
   single-char buffer that gets add()'d. Looking at the add() code, single-char
  : doesn't match any of the cases (., ,, [, (, ], ), -, +, @) so it falls
  through to Identifier. That's the correct behavior.

  Let me fix my Go port to match ‚ÄĒ remove the TokenColon special case:

‚óŹ Update(pkg/abaplint/lexer.go)

  failures ‚ÄĒ they're not lexer bugs, they're oracle file version mismatches. The

  version, the Go lexer runs on the other.

  go=1333 oracle=1333 (second run from different dir)

  - zif_vsp_service.intf.abap: same pattern

      115  
      116 +### Native Go ABAP Lexer ‚ÄĒ abaplint in Go                     
      117 +                                                              
      118 +The [abaplint](https://github.com/abaplint/abaplint) lexer has
          + been mechanically ported from TypeScript to native Go (`pkg/a
          +baplint`). This is the same lexer that powers abaplint ‚ÄĒ 48 to
          +ken types, all 6 lexer modes (normal, string, backtick, templa
          +te, comment, pragma), with full whitespace-context encoding.  
      119 +                                                              
      120 +**Verified via oracle-based differential testing** against the
          + real TypeScript abaplint:                                    
      121 +                                                              
      122 +```                                                           
      123 +=== DIFFERENTIAL KPI ===                                      
      124 +Files:   29/29 passed (100.0%)                                
      125 +Tokens:  22,612 total                                         
      126 +  Full match:  22,612 (100.0%)  ‚ÄĒ str + type + row + col      
      127 +  Str match:   22,612 (100.0%)                                
      128 +  Type match:  22,612 (100.0%)                                
      129 +  Pos match:   22,612 (100.0%)                                
      130 +```                                                           
      131 +                                                              
      132 +Zero dependencies, zero FFI. Pure Go, ~3.5M tokens/sec, ready 
          +for lint rules in Phase 2.                                    
      133 +                                                              
      134  ### ABAP LSP ‚ÄĒ Real-Time Diagnostics
      135  
      136  `vsp lsp --stdio` gives Claude Code (and other editors) **auto
           matic** error detection and navigation for ABAP files. No expl
           icit tool calls ‚ÄĒ the LSP pushes diagnostics on every save and
            compressed dependency context on file open.

       7 +## [2.31.0] - 2026-03-20                                       
       8 +### Features                                                   
       9 +                                                               
      10 +- **Native Go ABAP Lexer** (`pkg/abaplint`): Mechanical port of
         + the [abaplint](https://github.com/abaplint/abaplint) TypeScrip
         +t lexer to native Go. 48 token types, 6 lexer modes (normal, st
         +ring, backtick, template, comment, pragma), whitespace-context 
         +encoding. Oracle-verified: 100% match on 22,612 tokens across 2
         +9 ABAP files. ~3.5M tokens/sec, zero dependencies.             
      11 +- **Dependency Context Depth** (`pkg/ctxcomp`): `GetContext` no
         +w supports `depth` parameter (1-3) for multi-level dependency e
         +xpansion. Level 1 = direct deps (default), level 2 = deps of de
         +ps, level 3 = three levels deep. Tracks visited objects to avoi
         +d cycles, shares maxDeps budget across levels.                 
      12 +- **Oracle Differential Testing Framework** (`pkg/abaplint/test
         +data/oracle.js`): Node.js script runs the real TypeScript abapl
         +int on ABAP files, generates JSON fixtures. Go tests compare to
         +ken-by-token: string, type, row, col. Reports per-file and aggr
         +egate KPIs (str/type/pos match rates).                         
      13 +

‚óŹ 99.5% token match! The mismatches are two categories:

  1. Pragmas ‚ÄĒ abaplint strips ##PRAGMA tokens from statements (moves them to a
  separate pragmas list). Our splitter keeps them in. This is intentional in
  abaplint's removePragma().
  2. NativeSQL ‚ÄĒ The AMDP test class has embedded SQL that abaplint handles
  specially with NativeSQL statement type.

  Let me fix the pragma issue ‚ÄĒ it's the biggest one:

  these start with identifiers

       95 +// TestStatementMatcher_OracleDifferential compares Go stateme
          +nt TYPE classification against oracle.                        
       96 +func TestStatementMatcher_OracleDifferential(t *testing.T) {  
       97 +  fixtureData, err := os.ReadFile("testdata/oracle_stmts.json"
          +)                                                             
       98 +  if err != nil {                                             
       99 +    t.Skipf("oracle statement fixtures not found: %v", err)   
      100 +  }                                                           
      101 +                                                              
      102 +  var fixtures []oracleStmtFile                               
      103 +  if err := json.Unmarshal(fixtureData, &fixtures); err != nil
          + {                                                            
      104 +    t.Fatalf("parse oracle JSON: %v", err)                    
      105 +  }                                                           
      106 +                                                              
      107 +  sourceDirs := []string{                                     
      108 +    "../../embedded/abap",                                    
      109 +    "../../abap-adt-api/testdata/src",                        
      110 +    "../../abap/src",                                         
      111 +  }                                                           
      112 +                                                              
      113 +  lex := &Lexer{}                                             
      114 +  parser := &StatementParser{}                                
      115 +  matcher := NewStatementMatcher()                            
      116 +                                                              
      117 +  totalStmts := 0                                             
      118 +  typeMatches := 0                                            
      119 +  typeMismatches := make(map[string]int) // "got‚Üíexpected" ‚Üí c
          +ount                                                          
      120 +                                                              
      121 +  for _, fixture := range fixtures {                          
      122 +    source := findSourceFile(t, fixture.File, sourceDirs)     
      123 +    if source == "" {                                         
      124 +      continue                                                
      125 +    }                                                         
      126 +                                                              
      127 +    data, err := os.ReadFile(source)                          
      128 +    if err != nil {                                           
      129 +      continue                                                
      130 +    }                                                         
      131 +                                                              
      132 +    tokens := lex.Run(string(data))                           
      133 +    goStmts := parser.Parse(tokens)                           
      134 +    matcher.ClassifyStatements(goStmts)                       
      135 +    oracleStmts := fixture.Statements                         
      136 +                                                              
      137 +    minLen := len(goStmts)                                    
      138 +    if len(oracleStmts) < minLen {                            
      139 +      minLen = len(oracleStmts)                               
      140 +    }                                                         
      141 +                                                              
      142 +    for i := 0; i < minLen; i++ {                             
      143 +      totalStmts++                                            
      144 +      goType := goStmts[i].Type                               
      145 +      oType := oracleStmts[i].Type                            
      146 +                                                              
      147 +      if goType == oType {                                    
      148 +        typeMatches++                                         
      149 +      } else {                                                
      150 +        key := goType + "‚Üí" + oType                           
      151 +        typeMismatches[key]++                                 
      152 +      }                                                       
      153 +    }                                                         
      154 +  }                                                           
      155 +                                                              
      156 +  t.Logf("")                                                  
      157 +  t.Logf("=== STATEMENT TYPE KPI ===")                        
      158 +  t.Logf("Statements: %d total", totalStmts)                  
      159 +  t.Logf("Type match: %d (%.1f%%)", typeMatches, pct(typeMatch
          +es, totalStmts))                                              
      160 +  t.Logf("")                                                  
      161 +                                                              
      162 +  // Show top mismatches                                      
      163 +  type mismatch struct {                                      
      164 +    key   string                                              
      165 +    count int                                                 
      166 +  }                                                           
      167 +  var mm []mismatch                                           
      168 +  for k, v := range typeMismatches {                          
      169 +    mm = append(mm, mismatch{k, v})                           
      170 +  }                                                           
      171 +  // Sort by count desc                                       
      172 +  for i := 0; i < len(mm); i++ {                              
      173 +    for j := i + 1; j < len(mm); j++ {                        
      174 +      if mm[j].count > mm[i].count {                          
      175 +        mm[i], mm[j] = mm[j], mm[i]                           
      176 +      }                                                       
      177 +    }                                                         
      178 +  }                                                           
      179 +  t.Logf("Top mismatches (go‚Üíoracle):")                       
      180 +  for i, m := range mm {                                      
      181 +    if i >= 15 {                                              
      182 +      break

‚óŹ Now the big one ‚ÄĒ distinguish Call from Move. In abaplint, Call is a method
  call statement like lo_obj->method( ) or zcl_class=>method( ). Let me check
  what the actual patterns look like:

‚óŹ Bash(# Show some Call examples from oracle
      node -e "‚Ä¶)
  ‚éŅ ¬†assert_equals ( act = cut ->
     assert_equals ( act = in exp
     out -> write ( 'Hello world!'
     ‚Ä¶ +19 lines (ctrl+o to expand)
‚óŹ The key pattern for Call is: it's a statement that contains ->, =>, or ends
  with ( ) ‚ÄĒ it's a method call without an explicit assignment. In abaplint,
  Call is any statement that matches the Call statement pattern, which is
  essentially method/function calls that are NOT assignments.

  The simplest heuristic: if the statement doesn't contain = (not part of =>)
  before -> or =>, it's likely a Call. Let me add a proper Call detection:

‚óŹ Update(pkg/abaplint/matcher.go)
  ‚éŅ ¬†Added 5 lines, removed 9 lines
      227    sm.addKeyword("NativeSQL", "DECLARE", Seq(Str("DECLARE"), an
           yRest))
      228  
      229    // --- Fallback matchers (for Move and Call) ---
      230 -                                                              
      231 -  // Move: <target> = <source>  (assignment)                  
      232 -  // This is the catch-all for assignments                    
      233 -  sm.addFallback("Move", Seq(ident, Str("="), anyRest))       
      234 -  // Also handle field-symbol and component assignments: <fs>-
          -comp = ..., struct-comp = ...                                 
      230 +  // Call and Move both start with identifiers. The key distin
          +ction:                                                        
      231 +  // - Call: method/function call without assignment (no stand
          +alone = token)                                                
      232 +  // - Move: has an = assignment operator                     
      233 +  // We use a custom matcher that inspects tokens for = vs -> 
          +/ =>                                                          
      234 +  sm.addFallback("Call", callMatcher())                       
      235    sm.addFallback("Move", Seq(AnyToken(), anyRest)) // ultimate
            fallback
      236

          -tches all

‚óŹ Now add the callMatcher function:

‚óŹ Update(pkg/abaplint/matcher.go)
  ‚éŅ ¬†Added 59 lines
      237    _ = source
      238  }
      239  
      240 +// callMatcher returns a Matcher that detects method call stat
          +ements.                                                       
      241 +// A Call statement is one that contains method invocations (-
          +> => or function calls)                                       
      242 +// but does NOT have a top-level assignment (= that isn't part
          + of => or keyword params).                                    
      243 +func callMatcher() Matcher {                                  
      244 +  return func(tokens []Token, positions []int) []int {        
      245 +    var result []int                                          
      246 +    for _, pos := range positions {                           
      247 +      if pos < len(tokens) && isCallStatement(tokens[pos:]) { 
      248 +        result = append(result, len(tokens)) // consume all   
      249 +      }                                                       
      250 +    }                                                         
      251 +    return result                                             
      252 +  }                                                           
      253 +}                                                             
      254 +                                                              
      255 +func isCallStatement(tokens []Token) bool {                   
      256 +  if len(tokens) == 0 {                                       
      257 +    return false                                              
      258 +  }                                                           
      259 +                                                              
      260 +  // A Call statement has no top-level = assignment.          
      261 +  // Look for = that is NOT part of => and NOT a keyword param
          +eter (EXPORTING x =).                                         
      262 +  // If we find a standalone = before any -> or =>, it's likel
          +y Move.                                                       
      263 +  hasArrow := false                                           
      264 +  hasParenCall := false                                       
      265 +  parenDepth := 0                                             
      266 +                                                              
      267 +  for i, tok := range tokens {                                
      268 +    switch {                                                  
      269 +    case tok.Type == TokenInstanceArrow || tok.Type == TokenIn
          +stanceArrowW ||                                               
      270 +      tok.Type == TokenWInstanceArrow || tok.Type == TokenWIns
          +tanceArrowW ||                                                
      271 +      tok.Type == TokenStaticArrow || tok.Type == TokenStaticA
          +rrowW ||                                                      
      272 +      tok.Type == TokenWStaticArrow || tok.Type == TokenWStati
          +cArrowW:                                                      
      273 +      hasArrow = true                                         
      274 +    case tok.Str == "(":                                      
      275 +      parenDepth++                                            
      276 +    case tok.Str == ")":                                      
      277 +      parenDepth--                                            
      278 +    case tok.Type == TokenParenLeft || tok.Type == TokenParenL
          +eftW ||                                                       
      279 +      tok.Type == TokenWParenLeft || tok.Type == TokenWParenLe
          +ftW:                                                          
      280 +      parenDepth++                                            
      281 +      hasParenCall = true                                     
      282 +    case tok.Type == TokenParenRight || tok.Type == TokenParen
          +RightW ||                                                     
      283 +      tok.Type == TokenWParenRight || tok.Type == TokenWParenR
          +ightW:                                                        
      284 +      parenDepth--                                            
      285 +    case tok.Str == "=" && parenDepth == 0:                   
      286 +      // Check it's not part of =>                            
      287 +      if i+1 < len(tokens) && tokens[i+1].Str == ">" {        
      288 +        continue                                              
      289 +      }                                                       
      290 +      // Standalone = at top level ‚Üí this is Move, not Call   
      291 +      return false                                            
      292 +    }                                                         
      293 +  }                                                           
      294 +                                                              
      295 +  // It's a Call if it has arrows or paren calls and no top-le
          +vel assignment                                                
      296 +  return hasArrow || hasParenCall                             
      297 +}                                                             
      298 +

            a slice.
      300  func (sm *StatementMatcher) ClassifyStatements(stmts []Stateme
           nt) {
      301    for i := range stmts {

‚ĚĮ –Ņ—Ä–ĺ–ī–ĺ–Ľ–∂–į–Ķ–ľ, –į –≤ —á—Ď–ľ —Ä–į—Ā—Ö–ĺ–∂–ī–Ķ–Ĺ–ł–Ķ 99.97%?                                       

‚óŹ The 1 mismatch is the AMDP file zcl_adt_00_amdp_test.clas.abap ‚ÄĒ it has
  embedded SQLScript inside a METHOD ... BY DATABASE PROCEDURE:

  METHOD calculate_squares BY DATABASE PROCEDURE FOR HDB LANGUAGE SQLSCRIPT.
    DECLARE lv_i INTEGER;
    ...
    END WHILE;
  ENDMETHOD.

  abaplint has a special nativeSQL handler that detects METHOD ... BY DATABASE
  and treats everything inside as NativeSQL statements until ENDMETHOD. It then
  splits ENDMETHOD out as a separate statement even though the lexer doesn't see
   a period between the SQL and ENDMETHOD.

  Our splitter doesn't do this, so the SQL block + ENDMETHOD stay glued
  together, and the next ENDCLASS appears where abaplint expects ENDMETHOD ‚ÄĒ
  hence EndClass‚ÜíEndMethod.

  Let me port the NativeSQL handler.

  Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

‚óŹ Now let me check what the abaplint nativeSQL handler does exactly and look at
  the AMDP test file:

‚óŹ Bash(# Show the oracle's output for this specific file
      node -e "‚Ä¶)  ‚éŅ ¬†0 ClassDefinition | CLASS zcl_adt_00_amdp_test DEFINITION PUBLIC FINAL
      CREATE PUBLIC .
     1 Public | PUBLIC SECTION .
     ‚Ä¶ +26 lines (ctrl+o to expand)

‚óŹ Interesting ‚ÄĒ abaplint's NativeSQL handling is unusual here. The colon
  chaining inside the SQL block (from TYPES: earlier) is causing the SQL to get
  replicated. But the key point is: after METHOD ... BY DATABASE PROCEDURE,
  everything until ENDMETHOD becomes NativeSQL, and ENDMETHOD gets split out as
  its own statement.

  Let me add this post-processing step:

‚óŹ Update(pkg/abaplint/statements.go)
  ‚éŅ ¬†Added 70 lines
      130    }
      131  }
      132  
      133 +// nativeSQL post-processes statements to handle embedded SQL 
          +blocks.                                                       
      134 +// After METHOD ... BY DATABASE, all statements until ENDMETHO
          +D become NativeSQL.                                           
      135 +// If ENDMETHOD tokens are glued onto the last SQL statement, 
          +they get split out.                                           
      136 +// This matches abaplint's nativeSQL() method in statement_par
          +ser.ts.                                                       
      137 +func nativeSQL(stmts []Statement) []Statement {               
      138 +  var result []Statement                                      
      139 +  sql := false                                                
      140 +                                                              
      141 +  for i := 0; i < len(stmts); i++ {                           
      142 +    stmt := stmts[i]                                          
      143 +                                                              
      144 +    if !sql {                                                 
      145 +      // Check if this is METHOD ... BY DATABASE              
      146 +      if isMethodByDatabase(stmt) {                           
      147 +        sql = true                                            
      148 +        result = append(result, stmt)                         
      149 +        continue                                              
      150 +      }                                                       
      151 +      result = append(result, stmt)                           
      152 +      continue                                                
      153 +    }                                                         
      154 +                                                              
      155 +    // In SQL mode                                            
      156 +    first := stmt.FirstTokenStr()                             
      157 +    if first == "ENDMETHOD" {                                 
      158 +      sql = false                                             
      159 +      result = append(result, stmt)                           
      160 +      continue                                                
      161 +    }                                                         
      162 +                                                              
      163 +    // Check if this statement ends with ENDMETHOD.           
      164 +    // If so, split ENDMETHOD out.                            
      165 +    tokens := stmt.Tokens                                     
      166 +    if len(tokens) >= 2 {                                     
      167 +      lastIdx := len(tokens) - 1                              
      168 +      // Last token should be "." (Punctuation)               
      169 +      // Second-to-last should be "ENDMETHOD"                 
      170 +      if tokens[lastIdx].Type == TokenPunctuation && tokens[la
          +stIdx].Str == "." &&                                          
      171 +        toUpper(tokens[lastIdx-1].Str) == "ENDMETHOD" {       
      172 +        // Split: NativeSQL = tokens[0..lastIdx-2], EndMethod 
          += tokens[lastIdx-1..lastIdx]                                  
      173 +        sqlTokens := tokens[:lastIdx-1]                       
      174 +        endTokens := tokens[lastIdx-1:]                       
      175 +                                                              
      176 +        if len(sqlTokens) > 0 {                               
      177 +          result = append(result, Statement{Tokens: sqlTokens,
          + Type: "NativeSQL"})                                          
      178 +        }                                                     
      179 +        result = append(result, Statement{Tokens: endTokens, T
          +ype: "Unknown"})                                              
      180 +        sql = false                                           
      181 +        continue                                              
      182 +      }                                                       
      183 +    }                                                         
      184 +                                                              
      185 +    // Regular SQL line                                       
      186 +    stmt.Type = "NativeSQL"                                   
      187 +    result = append(result, stmt)                             
      188 +  }                                                           
      189 +                                                              
      190 +  return result                                               
      191 +}                                                             
      192 +                                                              
      193 +func isMethodByDatabase(stmt Statement) bool {                
      194 +  // Look for "METHOD <name> BY DATABASE" pattern             
      195 +  for i, tok := range stmt.Tokens {                           
      196 +    if toUpper(tok.Str) == "DATABASE" && i >= 2 && toUpper(stm
          +t.Tokens[i-1].Str) == "BY" {                                  
      197 +      return true                                             
      198 +    }                                                         
      199 +  }                                                           
      200 +  return false                                                
      201 +}                                                             
      202 +                                                              
      203  // toUpper is a simple ASCII upper for ABAP keywords.
      204  func toUpper(s string) string {
      205    b := make([]byte, len(s))

      255 +// Expr lazily resolves an expression by name from the express
          +ionRegistry.                                                  
      256 +// This breaks circular dependencies between expressions.     
      257 +func Expr(name string) Matcher {                              
      258 +  var cached Matcher                                          
      259 +  return func(tokens []Token, positions []int) []int {        
      260 +    if cached == nil {                                        
      261 +      if factory, ok := expressionRegistry[name]; ok {        
      262 +        cached = factory()                                    
      263 +      } else {                                                
      264 +        // Unknown expression ‚ÄĒ match nothing                 
      265 +        return nil                                            
      266 +      }                                                       
      267 +    }                                                         
      268 +    return cached(tokens, positions)                          
      269 +  }                                                           
      270 +}                                                             
      271 +                                                              
      272 +// FailMatcher always fails to match (used for failCombinator/
          +failStar).                                                    
      273 +func FailMatcher() Matcher {                                  
      274 +  return func(tokens []Token, positions []int) []int {        
      275 +    return nil                                                
      276 +  }

      138 +// Convert reg(/pattern/) and regex(/pattern/) calls, handling
          + nested /                                                     
      139 +function convertRegexCalls(code, funcName) {                  
      140 +  let result = "";                                            
      141 +  let i = 0;                                                  
      142 +  while (i < code.length) {                                   
      143 +    const idx = code.indexOf(funcName + "(", i);              
      144 +    if (idx === -1) {                                         
      145 +      result += code.substring(i);                            
      146 +      break;                                                  
      147 +    }                                                         
      148 +    // Check it's a word boundary                             
      149 +    if (idx > 0 && /\w/.test(code[idx - 1])) {                
      150 +      result += code.substring(i, idx + funcName.length);     
      151 +      i = idx + funcName.length;                              
      152 +      continue;                                               
      153 +    }                                                         
      154 +    result += code.substring(i, idx);                         
      155 +    // Find the opening /                                     
      156 +    let j = idx + funcName.length + 1; // skip "("            
      157 +    while (j < code.length && code[j] !== "/") j++;           
      158 +    if (j >= code.length) {                                   
      159 +      result += code.substring(idx);                          
      160 +      break;                                                  
      161 +    }                                                         
      162 +    j++; // skip opening /                                    
      163 +    // Find the closing / ‚ÄĒ it's the last / before the closing
          + )                                                            
      164 +    let lastSlash = -1;                                       
      165 +    let k = j;                                                
      166 +    let depth = 0;                                            
      167 +    while (k < code.length) {                                 
      168 +      if (code[k] === "/" && code[k - 1] !== "\\") lastSlash =
          + k;                                                           
      169 +      if (code[k] === ")") break;                             
      170 +      k++;                                                    
      171 +    }                                                         
      172 +    if (lastSlash === -1 || k >= code.length) {               
      173 +      result += code.substring(idx, k + 1);                   
      174 +      i = k + 1;                                              
      175 +      continue;                                               
      176 +    }                                                         
      177 +    const pattern = code.substring(j, lastSlash);             
      178 +    const escaped = pattern.replace(/\\/g, "\\\\").replace(/"/
          +g, '\\"');                                                    
      179 +    result += `Regex("${escaped}")`;                          
      180 +    i = k + 1; // skip the closing )                          
      181 +  }                                                           
      182 +  return result;                                              
      183 +}

      119    return "*" + tsType

      122 +func (t *transpiler) inferType(init *Node) string {           
      123 +  if init == nil {                                            
      124 +    return "interface{}"                                      
      125 +  }                                                           
      126 +  switch init.Kind {                                          
      127 +  case "NumericLiteral":                                      
      128 +    if strings.Contains(init.Value, ".") {                    
      129 +      return "float64"                                        
      130 +    }                                                         
      131 +    return "int"                                              
      132 +  case "StringLiteral":                                       
      133 +    return "string"                                           
      134 +  case "BooleanLiteral":                                      
      135 +    return "bool"                                             
      136 +  case "ArrayLiteral":                                        
      137 +    return "[]interface{}"                                    
      138 +  case "NullLiteral":                                         
      139 +    return "interface{}"                                      
      140 +  case "NewExpression":                                       
      141 +    return "*" + init.Name                                    
      142 +  case "PrefixUnaryExpression":                               
      143 +    // e.g., -1                                               
      144 +    return t.inferType(init.Expression)                       
      145 +  }                                                           
      146 +  return "interface{}"                                        
      147 +}                                                             
      148 +

      150    t.sb.WriteString(strings.Repeat("\t", t.indent))
      151    fmt.Fprintf(&t.sb, format, args...)

  –≠—ā–ĺ Layer 3 (structures) ‚ÄĒ hierarchical AST –Ņ–ĺ–≤–Ķ—Ä—Ö statements. –Ē–Ľ—Ź –Ķ–≥–ĺ –Ņ–ĺ—Ä—ā–į
  –Ĺ—É–∂–Ĺ–ĺ:
  1. Layer 1: Lexer ‚úÖ (—É–∂–Ķ –Ņ–ĺ—Ä—ā–ł—Ä–ĺ–≤–į–Ĺ)
  2. Layer 2: Statements ‚úÖ (splitter + type matcher)
  3. Layer 3: Structures (~1,700 lines TS) ‚ÄĒ –Ĺ—É–∂–Ķ–Ĺ –Ņ–ĺ—Ä—ā
  4. AST tree walking API (findAllStructures, findFirstExpression, etc.)
  5. –°–į–ľ–ł –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–į

  –Ě–ĺ –Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ā—ā—č–Ķ –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–į –Ĺ–Ķ —ā—Ä–Ķ–Ī—É—é—ā –Ņ–ĺ–Ľ–Ĺ–ĺ–≥–ĺ AST:

  ‚ĒĆ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēź

  –ź —ā–Ķ–Ņ–Ķ—Ä—Ć –ĺ—ā–≤–Ķ—ā –Ĺ–į —ā–≤–ĺ–Ļ –≤–ĺ–Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ā ‚ÄĒ –ľ–ĺ–∂–Ĺ–ĺ –Ľ–ł –ĺ—ā–ī–Ķ–Ľ–ł—ā—Ć –ī–į–Ĺ–Ĺ—č–Ķ –ĺ—ā –ļ–ĺ–ī–į?

  –ź preferred_compare_operator:

  ["EQ","NE","GT","LT","GE","LE","><"]}

  –Ē–į, –ľ–ĺ–∂–Ĺ–ĺ —Ā–ī–Ķ–Ľ–į—ā—Ć –ī–Ķ–ļ–Ľ–į—Ä–į—ā–ł–≤–Ĺ—č–Ļ DSL. –Ē–Ľ—Ź 89 –Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ā—ā—č—Ö –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ –Ņ–į—ā—ā–Ķ—Ä–Ĺ –ĺ–ī–ł–Ĺ:

  type Rule struct {
      Key         string
      Level       string            // "line", "statement", "token"  
      Match       func(stmt) bool   // –ļ–į–ļ–ł–Ķ —Ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ—ā–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—ā—č –Ņ—Ä–ĺ–≤–Ķ—Ä—Ź—ā—Ć
      Check       func(stmt) *Issue // –Ľ–ĺ–≥–ł–ļ–į –Ņ—Ä–ĺ–≤–Ķ—Ä–ļ–ł
      Config      map[string]any    // –Ĺ–į—Ā—ā—Ä–ĺ–Ļ–ļ–ł
  }

  –Ě–ĺ –≤–ľ–Ķ—Ā—ā–ĺ TS‚ÜíGo —ā—Ä–į–Ĺ—Ā–Ņ–ł–Ľ—Ź—Ü–ł–ł –ļ–į–∂–ī–ĺ–≥–ĺ –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–į, –ľ–ĺ–∂–Ĺ–ĺ –ł–∑–≤–Ľ–Ķ—á—Ć –ļ–ĺ–Ĺ—Ą–ł–≥–ł + –Ņ–į—ā—ā–Ķ—Ä–Ĺ—č
   –ł–∑ TS –ł —Ā–ī–Ķ–Ľ–į—ā—Ć Go runtime:

  // –Ē–Ķ–ļ–Ľ–į—Ä–į—ā–ł–≤–Ĺ–ĺ–Ķ –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–ĺ –≤ JSON/YAML
  rules:
    - key: line_length
      level: line
      check: "len(line) > config.length"
      config: {length: 120}

    - key: empty_statement
      level: statement
      check: "stmt.Type == 'Empty'"

    - key: obsolete_statement
      level: statement
      match: "stmt.FirstToken in 
  ['COMPUTE','ADD','SUBTRACT','MOVE','MULTIPLY','DIVIDE']"

  –Ě–ĺ —ć—ā–ĺ –Ī—É–ī–Ķ—ā —Ā–≤–ĺ–Ļ DSL ‚ÄĒ –ł —ć—ā–ĺ –Ī–ĺ–Ľ—Ć—ą–Ķ —Ä–į–Ī–ĺ—ā—č —á–Ķ–ľ –Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ā—ā–ĺ –Ņ—Ä–ĺ–≥–Ĺ–į—ā—Ć ts2go.

  –ü—Ä–į–≥–ľ–į—ā–ł—á–Ĺ—č–Ļ –Ņ—É—ā—Ć: ts2go –Ĺ–į 89 –Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ā—ā—č—Ö –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–į—Ö. –ě–Ĺ–ł —ą–į–Ī–Ľ–ĺ–Ĺ–Ĺ—č–Ķ, ts2go —É–∂–Ķ
  –≥–Ķ–Ĺ–Ķ—Ä–ł—ā valid Go. –Ě—É–∂–Ķ–Ĺ —ā–ĺ–Ľ—Ć–ļ–ĺ —ā–ĺ–Ĺ–ļ–ł–Ļ runtime layer (ABAPFile, Issue,
  getStatements(), getTokens()).

  –Ē–Ķ–Ľ–į–Ķ–ľ?

‚úĽ Brewed for 2m 1s

‚ĚĮ –ī–Ķ–Ľ–į–Ķ–ľ, –Ĺ–ĺ —á—ā–ĺ —Ā –ĺ—ā—Ā—ā–į–Ľ—Ć–Ĺ—č–ľ–ł –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–į–ľ–ł?                                       

‚óŹ –ě—Ā—ā–į–Ľ—Ć–Ĺ—č–Ķ 94 –Ņ—Ä–į–≤–ł–Ľ–į (24 —Ā—Ä–Ķ–ī–Ĺ–ł—Ö + 70 —Ā–Ľ–ĺ–∂–Ĺ—č—Ö) ‚ÄĒ –≤—Ā–Ķ –ł—Ā–Ņ–ĺ–Ľ—Ć–∑—É—é—ā AST tree
  walking. –Ě–ĺ –Ņ–ĺ—Ā–ľ–ĺ—ā—Ä–ł —á—ā–ĺ –ł–ľ —Ä–Ķ–į–Ľ—Ć–Ĺ–ĺ –Ĺ—É–∂–Ĺ–ĺ:

  –°—Ä–Ķ–ī–Ĺ–ł–Ķ (24) –ł—Ā–Ņ–ĺ–Ľ—Ć–∑—É—é—ā findFirstExpression/findAllExpressions ‚ÄĒ —ć—ā–ĺ –Ņ–ĺ–ł—Ā–ļ –Ņ–ĺ

      126 +  File       string            `json:"file"`                  
      127 +  IssueCount int               `json:"issue_count"`           
      128 +  Issues     []oracleLintIssue `json:"issues"`                
      129 +}                                                             
      130 +                                                              
      131 +type oracleLintIssue struct {                                 
      132 +  Key     string `json:"key"`                                 
      133 +  Message string `json:"message"`                             
      134 +  Row     int    `json:"row"`                                 
      135 +  Col     int    `json:"col"`                                 
      136 +}                                                             
      137 +                                                              
      138 +// TestLinter_OracleDifferential compares Go linter output aga
          +inst TypeScript abaplint oracle.                              
      139 +// Compares only rules that both implement: empty_statement, o
          +bsolete_statement,                                            
      140 +// preferred_compare_operator, line_length, max_one_statement.
      141 +func TestLinter_OracleDifferential(t *testing.T) {            
      142 +  fixtureData, err := os.ReadFile("testdata/oracle_lint.json")
      143 +  if err != nil {                                             
      144 +    t.Skipf("oracle lint fixtures not found: %v", err)        
      145 +  }                                                           
      146 +                                                              
      147 +  var fixtures []oracleLintFile                               
      148 +  if err := json.Unmarshal(fixtureData, &fixtures); err != nil
          + {                                                            
      149 +    t.Fatalf("parse oracle JSON: %v", err)                    
      150 +  }                                                           
      151 +                                                              
      152 +  // Use only the rules that match oracle config              
      153 +  goLinter := &Linter{Rules: []Rule{                          
      154 +    &LineLengthRule{MaxLength: 120},                          
      155 +    &EmptyStatementRule{},                                    
      156 +    &ObsoleteStatementRule{                                   
      157 +      Compute: true, Add: true, Subtract: true,               
      158 +      Multiply: true, Divide: true, Move: true, Refresh: true,
      159 +    },                                                        
      160 +    &MaxOneStatementRule{},                                   
      161 +    &PreferredCompareOperatorRule{                            
      162 +      BadOperators: []string{"EQ", "><", "NE", "GE", "GT", "LT
          +", "LE"},                                                     
      163 +    },                                                        
      164 +  }}                                                          
      165 +                                                              
      166 +  sharedRules := map[string]bool{                             
      167 +    "empty_statement":            true,                       
      168 +    "obsolete_statement":         true,                       
      169 +    "preferred_compare_operator": true,                       
      170 +    "line_length":                true,                       
      171 +    "max_one_statement":          true,                       
      172 +  }                                                           
      173 +                                                              
      174 +  sourceDirs := []string{                                     
      175 +    "../../embedded/abap",                                    
      176 +    "../../abap-adt-api/testdata/src",                        
      177 +    "../../abap/src",                                         
      178 +  }                                                           
      179 +                                                              
      180 +  totalOracle := 0                                            
      181 +  totalGo := 0                                                
      182 +  matchedByKey := 0    // oracle issue found in Go output (sam
          +e key+row)                                                    
      183 +  goOnlyByKey := 0     // Go found but oracle didn't          
      184 +  oracleOnlyByKey := 0 // oracle found but Go didn't          
      185 +  totalFiles := 0                                             
      186 +  passedFiles := 0                                            
      187 +  perRule := map[string][3]int{} // [matched, goOnly, oracleOn
          +ly]                                                           
      188 +                                                              
      189 +  for _, fixture := range fixtures {                          
      190 +    source := findSourceFile(t, fixture.File, sourceDirs)     
      191 +    if source == "" {                                         
      192 +      continue                                                
      193 +    }                                                         
      194 +    totalFiles++                                              
      195 +                                                              
      196 +    data, err := os.ReadFile(source)                          
      197 +    if err != nil {                                           
      198 +      continue                                                
      199 +    }                                                         
      200 +                                                              
      201 +    goIssues := goLinter.Run(filepath.Base(source), string(dat
          +a))                                                           
      202 +                                                              
      203 +    // Filter to shared rules                                 
      204 +    oracleSet := map[string]map[int]bool{} // key ‚Üí set of row
          +s                                                             
      205 +    for _, oi := range fixture.Issues {                       
      206 +      if !sharedRules[oi.Key] {                               
      207 +        continue                                              
      208 +      }                                                       
      209 +      totalOracle++                                           
      210 +      if oracleSet[oi.Key] == nil {                           
      211 +        oracleSet[oi.Key] = map[int]bool{}                    
      212 +      }                                                       
      213 +      oracleSet[oi.Key][oi.Row] = true                        
      214 +    }                                                         
      215 +                                                              
      216 +    goSet := map[string]map[int]bool{}                        
      217 +    for _, gi := range goIssues {                             
      218 +      if !sharedRules[gi.Key] {                               
      219 +        continue                                              
      220 +      }                                                       
      221 +      totalGo++                                               
      222 +      if goSet[gi.Key] == nil {                               
      223 +        goSet[gi.Key] = map[int]bool{}                        
      224 +      }                                                       
      225 +      goSet[gi.Key][gi.Row] = true                            
      226 +    }                                                         
      227 +                                                              
      228 +    fileMatch := 0                                            
      229 +    fileGoOnly := 0                                           
      230 +    fileOracleOnly := 0                                       
      231 +                                                              
      232 +    // Check Go issues against oracle                         
      233 +    for key, rows := range goSet {                            
      234 +      for row := range rows {                                 
      235 +        if oracleSet[key] != nil && oracleSet[key][row] {     
      236 +          matchedByKey++                                      
      237 +          fileMatch++                                         
      238 +          pr := perRule[key]                                  
      239 +          pr[0]++                                             
      240 +          perRule[key] = pr                                   
      241 +        } else {                                              
      242 +          goOnlyByKey++                                       
      243 +          fileGoOnly++                                        
      244 +          pr := perRule[key]                                  
      245 +          pr[1]++                                             
      246 +          perRule[key] = pr                                   
      247 +        }                                                     
      248 +      }                                                       
      249 +    }                                                         
      250 +                                                              
      251 +    // Check oracle issues not found by Go                    
      252 +    for key, rows := range oracleSet {                        
      253 +      for row := range rows {                                 
      254 +        if goSet[key] == nil || !goSet[key][row] {            
      255 +          oracleOnlyByKey++                                   
      256 +          fileOracleOnly++                                    
      257 +          pr := perRule[key]                                  
      258 +          pr[2]++                                             
      259 +          perRule[key] = pr                                   
      260 +        }                                                     
      261 +      }                                                       
      262 +    }                                                         
      263 +                                                              
      264 +    filePerfect := fileGoOnly == 0 && fileOracleOnly == 0     
      265 +    if filePerfect {                                          
      266 +      passedFiles++                                           
      267 +    }                                                         
      268 +                                                              
      269 +    status := "PASS"                                          
      270 +    if !filePerfect {                                         
      271 +      status = "FAIL"                                         
      272 +    }                                                         
      273 +                                                              
      274 +    oCount := 0                                               
      275 +    for _, rows := range oracleSet {                          
      276 +      oCount += len(rows)                                     
      277 +    }                                                         
      278 +    gCount := 0                                               
      279 +    for _, rows := range goSet {                              
      280 +      gCount += len(rows)                                     
      281 +    }                                                         
      282 +                                                              
      283 +    if !filePerfect {                                         
      284 +      t.Logf("%s %s: oracle=%d go=%d matched=%d goOnly=%d orac
          +leOnly=%d",                                                   
      285 +        status, fixture.File, oCount, gCount, fileMatch, fileG
          +oOnly, fileOracleOnly)                                        
      286 +    }                                                         
      287 +  }                                                           
      288 +                                                              
      289 +  t.Logf("")                                                  
      290 +  t.Logf("=== LINTER DIFFERENTIAL KPI ===")                   
      291 +  t.Logf("Files:       %d/%d passed (%.1f%%)", passedFiles, to
          +talFiles, pct(passedFiles, totalFiles))                       
      292 +  t.Logf("Oracle issues: %d", totalOracle)                    
      293 +  t.Logf("Go issues:     %d", totalGo)                        
      294 +  t.Logf("Matched (key+row): %d (%.1f%% of oracle)", matchedBy
          +Key, pct(matchedByKey, totalOracle))                          
      295 +  t.Logf("Go-only:     %d", goOnlyByKey)                      
      296 +  t.Logf("Oracle-only: %d", oracleOnlyByKey)                  
      297 +  t.Logf("")                                                  
      298 +  t.Logf("Per-rule breakdown:")                               
      299 +  for key, counts := range perRule {                          
      300 +    t.Logf("  %-30s matched=%d goOnly=%d oracleOnly=%d", key, 
          +counts[0], counts[1], counts[2])                              
      301 +  }                                                           
      302 +}                                                             
      303 +                                                              
      304  func BenchmarkLinter(b *testing.B) {
      305    data, err := os.ReadFile("../../embedded/abap/zcl_vsp_apc_ha
           ndler.clas.abap")
      306    if err != nil {

‚óŹ Default config has same operators. But oracle found 0 issues? That means
  abaplint's preferred_compare_operator checks expression-level matching, not
  just token presence. It only flags when the token is actually used as a
  comparison operator in the AST ‚ÄĒ not when "EQ" appears as part of an
  identifier or string.

  The file zapidummytestprog1 probably has things like TYPES: eq TYPE i. or
  method names containing "EQ". For proper matching we'd need Expression-level
  parsing. For now, let's just disable this rule in the oracle comparison since
  it needs AST expressions:
